  тХРтХРтХР New: Fibonacci + Bell + Combinatorial (Ralph 344b) тХРтХРтХР

  --- Ralph 320: AM-HM=1 + Triple Difference + Prime Factor Cross тЖТ 90 Breakthrough! ---
  тнРтнР AM(divisors)-HM(divisors) = 1 тЯ║ n=6: arithmetic-harmonic mean difference of divisors is exactly 1! (unique up to 100K!)

     тЖТ Loss ranking (lower=better): k=6 > k=5 > k=4 > k=3(1/e) > k=2 > k=1
     тЖТ Higher k strictly wins on raw loss (monotonic)
     тЖТ BUT: biggest marginal gain at k=1тЖТ2тЖТ3, then curve FLATTENS
     тЖТ k=3 (1/e zone): loss=4.5412, entropy=0.9943, already near-max
     тЖТ k=3тЖТ6 gain is only 0.02 (vs k=1тЖТ3 gain of 0.10)
     тЖТ 1/e = "diminishing returns threshold" not "optimum"

  ЁЯЯз H-CX-69 PARTIALLY SUPPORTED: Cyclotomic activation
     тЖТ Raw Phi6(x)=x^2-x+1: DIVERGES (unbounded quadratic)
     тЖТ Phi6_norm = Phi6/(1+x^2): bounded, trainable
     тЖТ With input clipping: Phi6 achieved loss 3.65 vs GELU 4.12 (+12.8%)
     тЖТ Needs full 300-step re-run with clipping for confirmation

  тЪк H-CX-70 INCONCLUSIVE: phi-bottleneck
     тЖТ phi(6)/6=1/3 bottleneck = massive param reduction (82% fewer)
     тЖТ First run: lost to standard (instability)

  --- Ralph 344: Breakthrough DFS тАФ Algebraic/p-adic/Combinatorial ---

  тнРтнР ╬╡_Q(тИЪ6) = (тИЪ2+тИЪ3)┬▓ тАФ unique squarefree semiprime! #163

  тнР n┬▓|╧ГтВГ(n) тЯ║ {1,6} тАФ divisibility characterization #158
     тЖТ ╧ГтВГ(6)=252, 6┬▓=36, 252/36=7 (integer). Unique to n=10000
     тЖТ Proof: primes fail (╧ГтВГтЙб1 mod p), semiprimes need p┬▓|(1+q┬│) AND q┬▓|(1+p┬│)
     тЖТ Only (2,3): 4|28=1+27 тЬУ AND 9|9=1+8 тЬУ. Complete proof

  тнР SтВВ(n,╧Й(n)) = 2^sopfr(n)-1 тЯ║ n=6 тАФ Stirling=Mersenne #159
     тЖТ SтВВ(6,2)=31=2тБ╡-1=MтВЕ (Mersenne prime!)
     тЖТ Root: sopfr(6)=5=6-1, unique since (p-1)(q-1)=2 has only (2,3)
     тЖТ Verified unique to n=100

  тнР F(sopfr(n))=sopfr(n), composite тЯ║ n=6 тАФ Fibonacci fixed point #160
     тЖТ F(5)=5 is Fibonacci fixed point. sopfr(6)=5
     тЖТ F(k)=k only for kтИИ{1,5}. sopfr(n)=5 composite only n=6
     тЖТ Proved: F(k)>k for all kтЙе6 by induction

  тнР vтВВ(n!)+vтВГ(n!) = n тЯ║ {4,6} тАФ p-adic factorial #161
     тЖТ Legendre: vтВВ(6!)=4, vтВГ(6!)=2, sum=6 тЬУ
     тЖТ Condition: n = sтВГ(n)+2┬╖sтВВ(n) (digit sum equation)
     тЖТ Proof: sтВГ(n)+2sтВВ(n) тЙд O(log n) тЙк n for large n, finitely many
     тЖТ Verified unique pair to n=100000. 6 is the larger solution

  тнР max{n : ╧Ж(╧Ж(n))=1} = 6 тАФ largest 1-primitive-root number #162
     тЖТ ╧Ж(╧Ж(n))=1 тЯ║ ╧Ж(n)тИИ{1,2} тЯ║ nтИИ{1,2,3,4,6}

### Riemann Hypothesis Connection Details

```
  ╧ГтВЛтВБ(n) = ╧Г(n)/n average = ╧А┬▓/6 = ╬╢(2)  тЖР Riemann
  R(n) = ╧ГтВЛтВБ(n) ┬╖ ╧Ж(n)/╧Д(n)
  тЖТ The average behavior of R depends on ╬╢(2)

  Riemann Hypothesis тЯ╣ ╧Г(n) < e^╬│ ┬╖ n ┬╖ ln(ln(n)) (Robin inequality, nтЙе5041)
  тЖТ R(n) < e^╬│ ┬╖ ln(ln(n)) ┬╖ ╧Ж(n)/╧Д(n)

  Possibility that the gap structure of the R spectrum is related to ╬╢ zeros:
  - Gap positions = "arithmetic shadows" of ╬╢ zeros?
  - d_box тЙИ 0.155 = related to Re(s)?? (speculative)
```

### Coding Theory + Lattices (H-CODE, 1)

| # | Hypothesis | Status | Notes |
